           ... -> output
      }
      (2): nn.CAddTable
    }
  }
  (5): cudnn.SpatialBatchNormalization
  (6): cudnn.ReLU
  (7): cudnn.SpatialAveragePooling(8x8, 1,1)
  (8): nn.View(64)
  (9): nn.Linear(64 -> 100)
}
Network has	75	convolutions
